## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time (t) and current population (P). This is a classic population dynamics problem where growth rate depends on population size through various density-dependent and density-independent mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Exponential (Malthusian) growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Density-independent growth where rate is proportional to population size'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population size'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Growth with minimum viable population threshold (strong Allee effect)'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Growth as balance between anabolism and catabolism with different scaling'}
- {'name': 'Power-law growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Generalized density-dependent growth with fractional scaling'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Flexible asymmetric sigmoidal growth model'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2', 'scenario': 'Linear and quadratic population feedback terms'}
- {'name': 'Time-varying exponential growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate with exponentially changing environment'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous analog', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Saturating reproduction minus density-dependent mortality'}
- {'name': 'Logistic with time-dependent carrying capacity', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t))', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth in a changing environment'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation → multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) modifying growth term
- Allee effects (positive density dependence at low P) → additional factor (P - c) creating a growth minimum threshold
- Logarithmic feedback → log(c/P) or log(P) terms indicate Gompertz-type diminishing returns near carrying capacity
- Competing anabolism/catabolism → difference of power laws c0*P**a - c1*P**b with different exponents
- Constant harvesting or immigration → additive constant terms independent of P, e.g., dP_dt = f(P) + c0
- Time-explicit environmental forcing → multiplicative or additive functions of t (e.g., sin(c*t), exp(c*t)) modulating growth rate
- Saturating per-capita growth → rational functions like c0/(1+c1*P) for per-capita rate, yielding c0*P/(1+c1*P) for total rate
- Cubic population terms → P*(P-c1)*(c2-P) patterns indicate bistability or strong Allee dynamics

Polynomial division: $P^3c_0/(P+c_2) = c_0P^2 - c_0c_2P + c_0c_2^2 - c_0c_2^3/(P+c_2)$
Plus $Pc_1/(P+c_2) = c_1 - c_1c_2/(P+c_2)$

Total: $c_0P^2 - c_0c_2P + c_0c_2^2 + c_1 - (c_0c_2^3+c_1c_2)/(P+c_2)$

GT: $-0.01095P^2 + 1.042P - 0.01623 + 0.002155/(P+0.1328)$

$c_0 = -0.01095$, $-c_0c_2 = 1.042 \Rightarrow c_2 = 95.16$... but then $c_0c_2^2 = -0.01095 \times 9055 = -99.15$, and $c_1 + c_0c_2^2 = -0.01623$, so $c_1 = 99.13$.

Check fraction: $-(c_0c_2^3 + c_1c_2)/(P+c_2) = -((-0.01095)(861878) + 99.13 \times 95.16)/(P+95.16)$
$= -(-9437.6 + 9432.7)/(P+95.16) = -(-4.9)/(P+95.16) = 4.9/(P+95.16)$

But GT needs $0.002155/(P+0.1328)$. These are different functions of P. **No match.**

Now let me check the remaining candidates more quickly:

**Candidates 1, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7**: Contain sin or log with polynomial - GT is rational. If we zero transcendental parts, remaining polynomial can't match rational GT. **No match.**

**Candidates 9, 10, 11, 12, 14**: Contain tanh/exp/sin/log combinations. **No match.**

**Candidate 32:** $-P(Pc_0-1) + c_1\tanh(Pc_2+c_3) = -c_0P^2 + P + c_1\tanh(...)$. Polynomial + tanh. **No match.**

**Candidate 33:** $P(Pc_0+1) + c_1\tanh(Pc_2+c_3) = c_0P^2 + P + c_1\tanh(...)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 34:** Has $t$ and tanh. **No match.**

**Candidate 35:** Has $t$ and sin. Can zero $t$ terms, but remaining is $P c_2 + c_3\sin(Pc_4+c_5)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 36:** $c_0\tanh(Pc_1+c_2) + c_3\exp(Pc_4)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 40-43:** Linear + tanh combinations. **No match.**

**Candidate 44:** $Pc_0 + Pc_1(Pc_2+1) + c_3\tanh(Pc_4) = c_1c_2P^2 + (c_0+c_1)P + c_3\tanh(Pc_4)$. Polynomial + tanh. **No match.**

**Candidate 45:** Same structure. **No match.**

**Candidate 46:** $P^2c_0 + Pc_1 + c_2\tanh(Pc_3)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 47:** $Pc_0(P+c_1) + c_2\tanh(Pc_3) = c_0P^2 + c_0c_1P + c_2\tanh(Pc_3)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 48:** $Pc_0 + c_1 + c_2\log(c_3\exp(Pc_4)+1)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 49-54:** Contain transcendental functions. **No match.**

**Candidate 58:** $c_0 + c_1\sin(Pc_2+c_3)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 59:** $Pc_0 + c_1\sin(c_2\log(Pc_3+1))$. **No match.**

**Candidate 62:** $P^2c_0 + c_1 + c_2\exp(Pc_3)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 64:** $Pc_0\log(Pc_1+1) + c_2\tanh(Pc_3)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 65:** $P^2c_0 + Pc_1 + c_2\exp(c_3 t)$. Has $t$. If $c_2=0$: quadratic polynomial. **No match.**

**Candidate 66:** $Pc_0(Pc_1+1) + c_2\exp(c_3 t)$. Same. **No match.**

**Candidate 69:** $c_0(P^2c_1 + Pc_2 + c_3)$. Quadratic polynomial. **No match.**

**Candidate 70-73, 75-79:** Quadratic polynomials or similar. GT is rational, not polynomial. **No match.**

**Candidate 78:** $P(c_0 + c_1|P|)$. With $P \geq 0$: $c_0P + c_1P^2$. Polynomial. **No match.**

**Candidate 80:** $(Pc_0 + c_1(P+c_2)\sin(c_3\log(Pc_4+1)))/(P+c_2)$
$= Pc_0/(P+c_2) + c_1\sin(c_3\log(Pc_4+1))$. Has sin(log(...)). **No match.**

**Candidate 81:** Has exp and log. **No match.**

**Candidate 83:** Has log(exp(...)) and log. **No match.**

**Candidate 84:** $Pc_0 + c_1\exp(P^{c_2}c_3)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 85:** $(P(Pc_0(P+c_1)+c_2) + c_3(P+c_1)\log(c_4\exp(Pc_5)+1))/(P+c_1)$
Zero log ($c_3=0$): $P(Pc_0(P+c_1)+c_2)/(P+c_1) = P^2c_0 + Pc_2/(P+c_1)$. Missing linear P. **No match.**

Let me also double-check **Candidate 29** more carefully:
$(P^2c_0(P+c_1) + Pc_2 + c_3(P+c_1)\log(Pc_4+1))/(P+c_1)$
Zero log: $(P^2c_0(P+c_1) + Pc_2)/(P+c_1) = P^2c_0 + Pc_2/(P+c_1)$
$= P^2c_0 + c_2 - c_1c_2/(P+c_1)$

This gives $P^2 + \text{const} + \text{const}/(P+c_1)$. Missing linear P term. **No match.**

Now let me verify **Candidate 60** again more carefully:
$(c_0 + (Pc_1+c_2)(P^2c_3+c_4))/(Pc_1+c_2)$
$= c_0/(Pc_1+c_2) + P^2c_3 + c_4$

GT partial fractions: $-0.01095P^2 + 1.042P - 0.01623 + 0.01623/(7.531P+1)$

Missing linear P. **No match.**

**Candidate 61:** $(P^2c_0(Pc_1+c_2) + Pc_3 + c_4)/(Pc_1+c_2)$
$= P^2c_0 + (Pc_3+c_4)/(Pc_1+c_2)$
$= P^2c_0 + c_3/c_1 + (c_4-c_2c_3/c_1)/(Pc_1+c_2)$

Missing linear P. **No match.**

Let me verify the matched candidates once more:

**Candidate 8:** $(P^3c_0+P^2c_1+Pc_2+c_3)/(P+c_4)$. GT = $(-0.08246P^3+7.836P^2+0.9198P)/(7.531P+1)$. Setting $c_4=1/7.531$, we need numerator $/7.531$. Set $c_3=0$. ✓ **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 56:** $P(P^2c_0+Pc_1+c_2)/(P+c_3)$. Same as GT form exactly. ✓ **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 23:** With log zeroed. ✓ **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 18:** With log zeroed. ✓ **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 31:** With $c_2=0$. ✓ **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 27:** With $c_3=2$. ✓ **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 28:** With $c_4=1$. ✓ **[MATCH]**

**Candidate 13:** With $c_4=2$, log zeroed. ✓ **[MATCH]**

Now let me also check **Candidate 29** with log NOT zeroed. We'd need $\log$ to provide the linear P term. But log is transcendental and can't produce a polynomial term. **No match.**

Let me also check **Candidate 30** with log not zeroed:
$P^2c_0 + Pc_2/(P+c_1) + c_3\log(Pc_4+1)$. Log can't match polynomial. **No match.**

**Candidate 85** with log not zeroed: $P^2c_0 + Pc_2/(P+c_1) + c_3\log(c_4\exp(Pc_5)+1)$. The softplus $\log(c_4\exp(Pc_5)+1)$ is not polynomial. **No match.**

Let me check **Candidate 17** with log not zeroed:
$(P(Pc_0(P+c_1)+c_2) + P^{c_3}c_4(P+c_1)\log(Pc_5+1))/(P+c_1)$
$= P^2c_0 + Pc_2/(P+c_1) + P^{c_3}c_4\log(Pc_5+1)$

The log term is transcendental. **No match.**

**Candidate 19** with log not zeroed:
$P(Pc_0 + c_2\log(Pc_3+1) + c_4/(P+c_1))$
$= c_0P^2 + c_2P\log(Pc_3+1) + Pc_4/(P+c_1)$
Has $P\log(...)$. **No match.**

**Candidate 25** with log not zeroed:
$Pc_0/(P+c_1) - P(Pc_2-1) + c_3\log(Pc_4+1)$
Has log. **No match.**

**Candidate 26** with log not zeroed:
$Pc_0/(P+c_3) + P^{c_1}c_2 + c_4\log(Pc_5+1)$
Has log. **No match.**

Now let me verify all remaining candidates I haven't explicitly checked:

**Candidate 34:** $Pc_0 + c_1\tanh(Pc_2+c_3) + c_4\sin(c_5 t+c_6) + c_7$. Zero $c_4$: $Pc_0 + c_1\tanh(...) + c_7$. Still has tanh. **No match.**

**Candidate 40:** $c_0(Pc_1 + c_2\tanh(Pc_3+c_4) + c_5) = c_0c_1P + c_0c_2\tanh(...) + c_0c_5$. **No match.**

**Candidate 41:** $c_0(Pc_1 + c_2(Pc_3 + c_4\tanh(Pc_5+c_6)) + c_7)$. Has tanh. **No match.**

**Candidate 43:** $Pc_0 + Pc_1 + c_2\tanh(Pc_3+c_4) + c_5 = (c_0+c_1)P + c_2\tanh(...) + c_5$. **No match.**

Now let me also check **Candidate 29** one more time with the full expression:
$(P^2c_0(P+c_1) + Pc_2 + c_3(P+c_1)\log(Pc_4+1))/(P+c_1)$

Expanding: $P^2c_0 + Pc_2/(P+c_1) + c_3\log(Pc_4+1)$

For this to match GT (rational function), we need $c_3\log(Pc_4+1) = \alpha P + \beta$ for all P, which is impossible. **No match.**

Summary of matches: Candidates 8, 13, 18, 23, 27, 28, 31, 56.

**Candidate 13:** Need $c_4=2$ (free constant). $c_5=0$ (zeroing log). Remaining: $Pc_0/(P+c_2) + c_1c_3P + c_1P^2$. ✓
**Candidate 18:** Need $c_4=0$ (zeroing log). Remaining: $c_0c_2P^2 + c_0P + c_3 - c_1c_3/(P+c_1)$. ✓
